  public Structured Encode(ICmptAltCnstPrntObjPrntOutpObject input)
    => _prntCnstPrntObjPrntOutp.Encode(input)
      .Add("alt", input.Alt.Encode());

  internal static CmptAltCnstPrntObjPrntOutpEncoder Factory(IEncoderRepository r) => new(r);

internal class CmptUnionAliasEncoder(
  IEncoderRepository encoders
) : IEncoder<ICmptUnionAlias>
{
  private readonly IEncoder<bool> _boolean = encoders.EncoderFor<bool>();
  private readonly IEncoder<decimal> _number = encoders.EncoderFor<decimal>();
  public Structured Encode(ICmptUnionAlias input)
    => input.HasA<bool>() ? _boolean.Encode(input.AsA<bool>())
     : input.HasA<decimal>() ? _number.Encode(input.AsA<decimal>())
     : Structured.Empty();

  internal static CmptUnionAliasEncoder Factory(IEncoderRepository r) => new(r);
}

     : Structured.Empty();
